5a3(1): po yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni/ tshad med pa'i thabs yang dag par rdzogs pa'o// lha'i dbang po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ shes rab tshad med pa

5b3(1): cad la phan pa nyid du bgyi ba dang / sems can thams cad la snying brtse ba nyid du bgyi ba dang / snying rje can du bgyi ba dang / snying brtse ba chen po nyid du bgyi ba dang / bsam pa thams cad

7a5(1): rang gi snying kha nas phyang ngo // a sho d+ha ne sho d+ha ne/ sar+b+ba pa paM bi sho d+ha ni/ shud+d+he bi shud+d+he/ sar+b+ba karma wa ra Na/ bi shud+d+he swa hA/ rig pa chen po 'di bshad ma thag tu/ sems can thams cad/
